<script>
        $(document).ready(function () {
            try {
                $(".jui-select").on("selectmenuchange", function (event, ui) {
                    try {
                        $(this).change();
                    } catch (x) { }
                });
            } catch (e) { /*console.log(e);*/ }
            $(".newletterEmailInput").val("");
            try {
                $('.num-input').keyup(validateNumber);
            } catch (e) { /*console.log(e);*/ }

            $(".btnTrackingModal").prop("disabled", false);
            $(".btnTrackingform").prop("disabled", false);
            if ($(".quick-cart-item").length > 0) {
                try {
                    DeleteNoItemInBasket();
                } catch (e) { }
            }
            try {
                $('.counter').counterUp({
                    delay: 10,
                    time: 2000
                });
            } catch (e) { }            
            if ($("#popup").length > 0) {
                $('#popup').modal('show');
                $(".newletterEmailInputpopUp").val("");
                $(".popup-form").validate({
                    rules: {
                        email: "required",
                    },
                });
                $(".popup-form").submit(function () {
                    if (!$(this).valid()) return false;
                    else
                        TrySendNewsletter("popUp");
                    $(".newletterEmailInputpopUp").bind("keyup", function () {
                        $(".newslerretEmaiLErrorpopUp").hide();
                        $(".newletterEmailInputpopUp").unbind("keyup");
                    })
                    return false;
                });
            }
        });
</script>
